type="application/ld+json">{"@context":{"@vocab":"http://schema.org","articleId":{"@id":"Text","@type":"@id"},"topics":{"@id":"Text","@type":"@id"}},"@type":"NewsArticle","headline":"Sam’s Club Membership Deal: How to join for just $15","url":"https://www.nbcnews.com/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230","thumbnailUrl":"https://media-cldnry.s-nbcnews.com/image/upload/t_social_share_1024x768_scale,f_auto,q_auto:best/rockcms/2024-08/240815-sams-club-explainer-vl-sq-d308c8.jpg","alternativeHeadline":"Sam's Club membership is on sale for $15: What you need to know","articleBody":"Shopping at Sam’s Club is all about getting the best deals on great products. Thinking about joining? Now’s the time: through Sept. 30, non-members can get a year-long Club membership for just $15 — that’s 70% off the regular price — or a Plus membership with even more benefits for $50 (over 50% off). Plus, current members can get extra perks through Sept. 30.  Here’s what you need to know. Through Sept. 30, non-members can get a year-long Sam’s Club membership for just $15, that’s 70% off the typical $50 membership price (terms apply). The Club tier gives you access to savings on gadgets, groceries, household essentials, fashion for the entire family and more. You also get perks like members-only deals and sales, same-day delivery and discounts on gas. Plus, Club members can now get free curbside pickup when you spend $50 or more on eligible items.  If you’re looking for even more ways to save, the Sam’s Club Plus membership comes with extra benefits and is on sale through Sept. 30, too: Non-members can get the upgraded tier for $50 for the year — that’s more than 50% off the usual $110 price (terms apply). One of the newest next-level perks is free Delivery from Club or free shipping, both on eligible orders of $50 or more. You’ll also get pharmacy savings and more cash back. No matter which membership you get, you’ll have access to other beloved perks including budget-friendly wedding services, travel savings, gift card deals, discounted home improvements and a robust auto-buying program. With a membership, you also get access to the retailer’s beloved Member’s Mark brand. (Shop some of our favorite picks below). Current Sam’s Club members aren’t left out either. Current club and Plus members can get extra perks through Sept. 30, including statement credits and special discounts (terms apply).  SKIP AHEAD  What are the different types of memberships? | Membership benefits | Plus membership benefits | Why trust NBC Select? What are the different types of Sam’s Club memberships? There are two levels of Sam’s Club memberships: the classic Sam’s Club membership and a Sam’s Club Plus membership.  The first tier is a year-long, base-level membership, which lets you shop for products in stores or online. It also comes with perks like access to exclusive sale events and fuel discounts. The Club membership typically costs $50, but is currently on sale for $15 for non-members through Sept. 30. The Sam’s Club Plus membership is usually $110 for a year, but is now on sale for $50 for non-members through Sept. 30. This premium and more robust membership is ideal for businesses, according to the brand. It offers all the Club tier perks plus additional ways to save including free shipping on orders $50 or over free Delivery from Club on qualifying orders as well as more cash back. What benefits come with a Sam’s Club membership? When you sign up for a basic Sam’s Club membership, now $15 (70% off) for non-members through Sept. 30, you get more than just bulk savings. With this annual membership (regularly $50), you’ll get these perks: Two complimentary membership cards: Each membership comes with a card for the account holder and one free card for another household member. Add up to eight members at a discounted rate.Members-only sales: Besides Sam’s Club reduced pricing, get access to Instant Savings events.Scan & Go shopping: When shopping in person, speed up the process by using this app to scan items, then easily pay directly in the app to skip the checkout lines. Just head right out with a digital receipt. Same-day delivery: Get same-day delivery on eligible items ordered by 1 p.m. There’s no order minimum for this service but a $12 fee per order for club members ($8 or free for orders over $50 for Plus members).Curbside pickup: Shop eligible items online or from the Sam’s Club app. Pick up the order at your local Sam's Club without getting out of the car. Just check in via your phone and a Sam's employee will load the order right into the car. Now, the $4 fee for this service it’s waived on orders over $50 (and it’s free for Plus members). Fuel and gift card savings: Sam’s Club members can use exclusive gas prices and save up to 25% off gift cards from favorite stores and brands. Health and wellness savings: Club members have access to free hearing tests, walk-in vaccines, hundreds of generic brand prescriptions starting at $4 and 40% off additional prescription glasses when you buy a complete pair.  What are the benefits of a Sam’s Club Plus membership? For those looking for the most savings, Sam’s Club Plus membership is the premium option. This next-level annual membership is on sale for $50 for non-members through Sept. 30 (normally $110 for the year). This upgraded membership comes with some additional benefits including:  Early shopping: Monday through Friday, Plus members can beat the crowds and shop two hours before the clubs open to all members. On Saturdays, shop one hour earlier, depending on location. Early access to sales events: Plus members get early access to online sales events and in-store deals. Extra cash back: All Club members earn 1% Sam’s Cash when they use a Sam’s Club Mastercard, but Plus members get 3%. For other payment methods, Plus members get 2% cash back on qualifying purchases (with a year max of $500).Same-day delivery: Now, Plus members get free same-day delivery on qualifying orders of $50 or more placed before 1 p.m. There’s an $8 service fee for orders under $50. Curbside pickup: Plus members can enjoy free curbside pickup (which is $4 for Club members on orders under $50). Tire and installation savings: Save 50% on tire installation with four-year roadside assistance and lifetime repair as a Plus member. Pharmacy savings: Get select generic prescription medications for $0 as a Plus member.  What limited time only perks can current Sam’s Club and Plus members get? Current Sam’s Club members can get new, limited time only rewards through Sept. 30. (Terms apply.) In-Club member-only limited time offers $50 statement credit: Members earn a $50 statement credit when they open a new credit account and use it to make $50 in eligible Sam’s Club purchases within the first 30 days. $20 off with upgrade to Plus: Members get $20 off $40 or more in eligible purchase when they upgrade to Plus in-club. $10 off with Scan & Go: Members who use Scan & Go for the first time get $10 off their basket when they scan a barcode in the club.  $5 off with a flu shot: Members get $5 off their basket when they get a flu shot and/or a Covid shot ($10 total — limit 1 per cardholder). Online member-only offers $50 statement credit: Members earn a $50 statement credit when they open a new credit account and use it to make $50 in eligible Sam’s Club purchases within the first 30 days. $20 in Sam’s Cash: Club members get $20 in Sam’s Cash when they upgrade to Plus online and spend $40 or more in eligible purchases online or in-club. $10 in Sam’s Cash: Members earn $10 Sam’s Cash when they order online and use Curbside Pickup, Delivery from Club, Express Delivery, or shipping for the first time.Up to $50 Sam’s Cash: Members get $10 Sam’s Cash for each friend that joins using the member’s referral link (limit of 5). Best Member’s Mark finds Member’s Mark is a brand of products offered exclusively at Sam’s Club. You can find food, home, pet supplies and more, all under the Member's Mark brand. Member’s Mark Musical Halloween Skeletons (Set of 2) Halloween is almost here, and these outdoor musical skeletons set the tone. The set includes two interactive skeleton musicians standing tall at 5 feet and 5 inches with LED eyes. These motion-activated maestros also play a spooky jazz duet and use an adaptor plug-in, so they can be used indoors or outdoors, depending on where you want to get the party started.  Member’s Mark 8-Piece Flip-lock Pantry Storage If your pantry needs some organization, this set of eight rectangle and square food containers doesn’t just save space, the containers help preserve freshness with flip-lock lids, per the brand. They have clear windows for an easy view, but the best part is the lids are interchangeable across boxes, so you don’t have to worry about matching them up to find the right fit.  Member’s Mark Women’s Shacket Layer up with this cozy (and versatile) shacket as the season gets colder. It’s made of recycled materials, according to the brand, and combines the relaxed fit of a shirt with the extra warmth of a jacket. This machine-washable comes in a range of sizes (XS-3XL), six plaid color combos, and matching options for the entire family in men’s, girls’ and boys’ styles.  Member’s Mark Hotel Premier Collection Premium Cooling Gel Memory Foam Pillow For hot sleepers, the right cooling pillow can be a worthwhile investment. Luckily, this Member’s Mark Member’s Mark Hotel Premier Collection Premium Cooling Gel Memory Foam Pillow is under $20. It also has a cool-to-the-touch, washable zip cover with an antimicrobial treatment that prevents odor-causing bacteria from growing, according to Sam's.  Member’s Mark Lindsey Modular Fabric Sofa with Storage Ottoman Upgrade your living space with a new place for loved ones to settle in. This plush sofa’s modular design means you can change the different pieces and connect the storage ottoman on either side to create a lounge that fits best in your space or use it as a separate coffee table/footrest. It comes in seven neutral, stain-resistant, water-repellant and pet-friendly fabrics. Member’s Mark 24-oz Stainless Steel Insulated Tumblers (2-pack) Available in four color combinations, this set of two stainless steel tumblers can help you up your water intake while cutting down on single-use plastics. The 24-ounce tumblers have double-wall vacuum insulation, which keeps hot drinks warm, cold drinks chilled and the bottle sweat-free, according to the brand. These cupholder-friendly tumblers also come with screw lids and stainless steel straws with silicone tips. Plus, the tumblers are BPA-free, says Sam's, and dishwasher-safe.  Member’s Mark Set of 2 Acacia Wood Charcuterie Boards Whether you’re gearing up for holiday entertaining or on the lookout for hostess gift ideas, check out this set of two charcuterie boards. Handmade from natural acacia wood, the rectangular and round serving pieces have a smooth finish and can be used for everything from meats and cheeses to desserts.  Member’s Mark Weekender Travel Bag From road trips to gifts they’ll actually use, there’s a reason this Weekender bag is a best-seller. This durable carry-on bag is made of linen and cotton and has a detachable shoulder strap. The roomy interior has a zipper pocket for cosmetics or small accessories and a separate bottom shoe compartment.  Member’s Mark 700-Thread-Count Sheet Set These wrinkle-free, 100% Egyptian cotton sheets are quick-drying and offer hotel-quality softness thanks to a high thread count, per the brand. They’re also a great choice for hot sleepers because the cotton material helps regulate body temperature while the bacteria-fighting finish helps keep them smelling fresh, according to the brand. They are available in eight neutral colors, like Soft Silver, Zinc or Washed Indigo and a range of sizes from twin to split king. Member’s Mark Women’s Everyday High-Rise Ankle Legging These size-inclusive leggings are made of four-way stretch fabric that’s UPF 50 and wicks away sweat, according to the brand, and they have two functional pockets for under $10. They also have a V-shaped waistline and hit right above the ankle.  Member’s Mark Kids’ Explorer Sofa For the youngest members on your holiday gift list, check out this durable play sofa that encourages imagination and grows with kiddos. The foldable couch comes in four separate foam pieces, giving little ones the versatility to arrange it into multiple creative shapes. There are seven colors to choose from, and the removable covers are machine-washable for easy cleaning. Member’s Mark 2-Piece Hardside Luggage Set This hardside luggage set covers you for long and short trips with a 20” carry-on and a 28” suitcase. Both bags have a scratch-resistant outer shell and come in five colors, according to the brand. The suitcases also have dual swivel wheels and TSA combination locks. Inside the carry-on bag, there’s a wet-dry and shoe pocket, and the larger suitcase also has an adjustable compression pad to help keep things from shifting. Why trust NBC Select? Here’s how to choose the best streaming service</a></h3></div></div></div></section></div><a href="/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230#anchor-WhatarethedifferenttypesofSamsClubmemberships" id="anchor-WhatarethedifferenttypesofSamsClubmemberships" class="scrollLink"><h2 class="">What are the different types of Sam’s Club memberships?</h2></a><p class="">There are two levels of Sam’s Club memberships: the classic Sam’s Club membership and a Sam’s Club Plus membership. </p><p class="">The first tier is a year-long, base-level membership, which lets you shop for products in stores or online. It also comes with perks like access to exclusive sale events and fuel discounts. The Club membership typically costs $50, but is currently on sale for $15 for non-members through Sept. 30.</p><p class="">The Sam’s Club Plus membership is usually $110 for a year, but is now on sale for $50 for non-members through Sept. 30. This premium and more robust membership is ideal for businesses, according to the brand. It offers all the Club tier perks plus additional ways to save including free shipping on orders $50 or over free Delivery from Club on qualifying orders as well as more cash back.</p><a href="/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230#anchor-WhatbenefitscomewithaSamsClubmembership" id="anchor-WhatbenefitscomewithaSamsClubmembership" class="scrollLink"><h2 class="">What benefits come with a Sam’s Club membership?</h2></a><p class="">When you sign up for a basic Sam’s Club membership, now $15 (70% off) for non-members through Sept. 30, you get more than just bulk savings. With this annual membership (regularly $50), you’ll get these perks:</p><ul class="break-above body-ul body-list-el"><li><strong>Two complimentary membership cards:</strong> Each membership comes with a card for the account holder and one free card for another household member. Add up to eight members at a discounted rate.</li><li><strong>Members-only sales: </strong>Besides Sam’s Club reduced pricing, get access to Instant Savings events.</li><li><strong>Scan & Go shopping: </strong>When shopping in person, speed up the process by using this app to scan items, then easily pay directly in the app to skip the checkout lines. Just head right out with a digital receipt. </li><li><strong>Same-day delivery: </strong>Get same-day delivery on eligible items ordered by 1 p.m. There’s no order minimum for this service but a $12 fee per order for club members ($8 or free for orders over $50 for Plus members).</li><li><strong>Curbside pickup: </strong>Shop eligible items online or from the Sam’s Club app. Pick up the order at your local Sam's Club without getting out of the car. Just check in via your phone and a Sam's employee will load the order right into the car. Now, the $4 fee for this service it’s waived on orders over $50 (and it’s free for Plus members). </li><li><strong>Fuel and gift card savings: </strong>Sam’s Club members can use exclusive gas prices and save up to 25% off gift cards from favorite stores and brands. </li><li><strong>Health and wellness savings:</strong> Club<strong> </strong>members have access to free hearing tests, walk-in vaccines, hundreds of generic brand prescriptions starting at $4 and 40% off additional prescription glasses when you buy a complete pair. </li></ul><a href="/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230#anchor-WhatarethebenefitsofaSamsClubPlusmembership" id="anchor-WhatarethebenefitsofaSamsClubPlusmembership" class="scrollLink"><h2 class="">What are the benefits of a Sam’s Club Plus membership?</h2></a><p class="">For those looking for the most savings, Sam’s Club Plus membership is the premium option. This next-level annual membership is on sale for $50 for non-members through Sept. 30 (normally $110 for the year). This upgraded membership comes with some additional benefits including: </p><ul class="break-above body-ul body-list-el"><li><strong>Early shopping: </strong>Monday through Friday, Plus members can beat the crowds and shop two hours before the clubs open to all members. On Saturdays, shop one hour earlier, depending on location. </li><li><strong>Early access to sales events: </strong>Plus members get early access to online sales events and in-store deals. </li><li><strong>Extra cash back: </strong>All Club members earn 1% Sam’s Cash when they use a Sam’s Club Mastercard, but Plus members get 3%. For other payment methods, Plus members get 2% cash back on qualifying purchases (with a year max of $500).</li><li><strong>Same-day delivery: </strong>Now, Plus members get free same-day delivery on qualifying orders of $50 or more placed before 1 p.m. There’s an $8 service fee for orders under $50. </li><li><strong>Curbside pickup: </strong>Plus members can enjoy free curbside pickup (which is $4 for Club members on orders under $50). </li><li><strong>Tire and installation savings: </strong>Save 50% on tire installation with four-year roadside assistance and lifetime repair as a Plus member. </li><li><strong>Pharmacy savings: </strong>Get select generic prescription medications for $0 as a Plus member. </li></ul><a href="/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230#anchor-WhatlimitedtimeonlyperkscancurrentSamsClubandPlusmembersget" id="anchor-WhatlimitedtimeonlyperkscancurrentSamsClubandPlusmembersget" class="scrollLink"><h2 class="">What limited time only perks can current Sam’s Club and Plus members get?</h2></a><p class="">Current Sam’s Club members can get new, limited time only rewards through Sept. 30. (Terms apply.)</p><a href="/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230#anchor-InClubmemberonlylimitedtimeoffers" id="anchor-InClubmemberonlylimitedtimeoffers" class="scrollLink"><h3 purchase when they <a data-commerce-encoding="true" data-seller-id="ncrg1185331" target="_blank">upgrade to Plus</a> in-club. </li><li><strong>$10 off with Scan & Go: </strong>Members who use Scan & Go for the first time get $10 off their basket when they scan a barcode in the club.  </li><li><strong>$5 off with a flu shot: </strong>Members get $5 off their basket when they get a flu shot and/or a Covid shot ($10 total — limit 1 per cardholder).</li></ul><a href="/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230#anchor-Onlinememberonlyoffers" id="anchor-Onlinememberonlyoffers" class="scrollLink"><h3 class="">Online member-only offers</h3></a><ul joins using the member’s referral link (limit of 5).</li></ul><a href="/select/shopping/sams-club-fall-membership-deal-rcna167230#anchor-BestMembersMarkfinds" id="anchor-BestMembersMarkfinds" Plus, current members get extra perks through Sept. 30.","content":{"text":["Shopping at Sam’s Club is all about getting the best deals on great products. Thinking about joining? Now’s the time: through Sept. 30, non-members can get a year-long Club membership for just $15 — that’s 70% off the regular price — or a Plus membership with even more benefits for $50 (over 50% off).","Plus, current members can get extra perks through Sept. 30. ","Here’s what you need to know.","Through Sept. 30, non-members can get a year-long Sam’s Club membership for just $15, that’s 70% off the typical $50 membership price (terms apply). The Club tier gives you access to savings on gadgets, groceries, household essentials, fashion for the entire family and more. You also get perks like members-only deals and sales, same-day delivery and discounts on gas. Plus, Club members can now get free curbside pickup when you spend $50 or more on eligible items. ","If you’re looking for even more ways to save, the Sam’s Club Plus membership comes with extra benefits and is on sale through Sept. 30, too: Non-members can get the upgraded tier for $50 for the year — that’s more than 50% off the usual $110 price (terms apply). One of the newest next-level perks is free Delivery from Club or free shipping, both on eligible orders of $50 or more. You’ll also get pharmacy savings and more cash back.","No matter which membership you get, you’ll have access to other beloved perks including budget-friendly wedding services, travel savings, gift card deals, discounted home improvements and a robust auto-buying program. With a membership, you also get access to the retailer’s beloved Member’s Mark brand. (Shop some of our favorite picks below).","Current Sam’s Club members aren’t left out either. Current club and Plus members can get extra perks through Sept. 30, including statement credits and special discounts (terms apply). ","SKIP AHEAD  What are the different types of memberships? | Membership benefits | Plus membership benefits | Why trust NBC Select?","What are the different types of Sam’s Club memberships?","There are two levels of Sam’s Club memberships: the classic Sam’s Club membership and a Sam’s Club Plus membership. ","The first tier is a year-long, base-level membership, which lets you shop for products in stores or online. It also comes with perks like access to exclusive sale events and fuel discounts. The Club membership typically costs $50, but is currently on sale for $15 for non-members through Sept. 30.","The Sam’s Club Plus membership is usually $110 for a year, but is now on sale for $50 for non-members through Sept. 30. This premium and more robust membership is ideal for businesses, according to the brand. It offers all the Club tier perks plus additional ways to save including free shipping on orders $50 or over free Delivery from Club on qualifying orders as well as more cash back.","What benefits come with a Sam’s Club membership?","When you sign up for a basic Sam’s Club membership, now $15 (70% off) for non-members through Sept. 30, you get more than just bulk savings. With this annual membership (regularly $50), you’ll get these perks:","Two complimentary membership cards: Each membership comes with a card for the account holder and one free card for another household member. Add up to eight members at a discounted rate.Members-only sales: Besides Sam’s Club reduced pricing, get access to Instant Savings events.Scan \u0026 Go shopping: When shopping in person, speed up the process by using this app to scan items, then easily pay directly in the app to skip the checkout lines. Just head right out with a digital receipt. Same-day delivery: Get same-day delivery on eligible items ordered by 1 p.m. There’s no order minimum for this service but a $12 fee per order for club members ($8 or free for orders over $50 for Plus members).Curbside pickup: Shop eligible items online or from the Sam’s Club app. Pick up the order at your local Sam's Club without getting out of the car. Just check in via your phone and a Sam's employee will load the order right into the car. Now, the $4 fee for this service it’s waived on orders over $50 (and it’s free for Plus members). Fuel and gift card savings: Sam’s Club members can use exclusive gas prices and save up to 25% off gift cards from favorite stores and brands. Health and wellness savings: Club members have access to free hearing tests, walk-in vaccines, hundreds of generic brand prescriptions starting at $4 and 40% off additional prescription glasses when you buy a complete pair. ","What are the benefits of a Sam’s Club Plus membership?","For those looking for the most savings, Sam’s Club Plus membership is the premium option. This next-level annual membership is on sale for $50 for non-members through Sept. 30 (normally $110 for the year). This upgraded membership comes with some additional benefits including: ","Early shopping: Monday through Friday, Plus members can beat the crowds and shop two hours before the clubs open to all members. On Saturdays, shop one hour earlier, depending on location. Early access to sales events: Plus members get early access to online sales events and in-store deals. Extra cash back: All Club members earn 1% Sam’s Cash when they use a Sam’s Club Mastercard, but Plus members get 3%. For other payment methods, Plus members get 2% cash back on qualifying purchases (with a year max of $500).Same-day delivery: Now, Plus members get free same-day delivery on qualifying orders of $50 or more placed before 1 p.m. There’s an $8 service fee for orders under $50. Curbside pickup: Plus members can enjoy free curbside pickup (which is $4 for Club members on orders under $50). Tire and installation savings: Save 50% on tire installation with four-year roadside assistance and lifetime repair as a Plus member. Pharmacy savings: Get select generic prescription medications for $0 as a Plus member. ","What limited time only perks can current Sam’s Club and Plus members get?","Current Sam’s Club members can get new, limited time only rewards through Sept. 30. (Terms apply.)","In-Club member-only limited time offers","$50 statement credit: Members earn a $50 statement credit when they open a new credit account and use it to make $50 in eligible Sam’s Club purchases within the first 30 days. $20 off with upgrade to Plus: Members get $20 off $40 or more in eligible purchase when they upgrade to Plus in-club. $10 off with Scan \u0026 Go: Members who use Scan \u0026 Go for the first time get $10 off their basket when they scan a barcode in the club.  $5 off with a flu shot: Members get $5 off their basket when they get a flu shot and/or a Covid shot ($10 total — limit 1 per cardholder).","Online member-only offers","$50 statement credit: Members earn a $50 statement credit when they open a new credit account and use it to make $50 in eligible Sam’s Club purchases within the first 30 days. $20 in Sam’s Cash: Club members get $20 in Sam’s Cash when they upgrade to Plus online and spend $40 or more in eligible purchases online or in-club. $10 in Sam’s Cash: Members earn $10 Sam’s Cash when they order online and use Curbside Pickup, Delivery from Club, Express Delivery, or shipping for the first time.Up to $50 Sam’s Cash: Members get $10 Sam’s Cash for each friend that joins using the member’s referral link (limit of 5).","Best Member’s Mark finds","Member’s Mark is a brand of products offered exclusively at Sam’s Club. You can find food, home, pet supplies and more, all under the Member's Mark brand.","Member’s Mark Musical Halloween Skeletons (Set of 2)","Halloween is almost here, and these outdoor musical skeletons set the tone. The set includes two interactive skeleton musicians standing tall at 5 feet and 5 inches with LED eyes. These motion-activated maestros also play a spooky jazz duet and use an adaptor plug-in, so they can be used indoors or outdoors, depending on where you want to get the party started. ","Member’s Mark 8-Piece Flip-lock Pantry Storage","If your pantry needs some organization, this set of eight rectangle and square food containers doesn’t just save space, the containers help preserve freshness with flip-lock lids, per the brand. They have clear windows for an easy view, but the best part is the lids are interchangeable across boxes, so you don’t have to worry about matching them up to find the right fit. ","Member’s Mark Women’s Shacket","Layer up with this cozy (and versatile) shacket as the season gets colder. It’s made of recycled materials, according to the brand, and combines the relaxed fit of a shirt with the extra warmth of a jacket. This machine-washable comes in a range of sizes (XS-3XL), six plaid color combos, and matching options for the entire family in men’s, girls’ and boys’ styles. ","Member’s Mark Hotel Premier Collection Premium Cooling Gel Memory Foam Pillow","For hot sleepers, the right cooling pillow can be a worthwhile investment. Luckily, this Member’s Mark Member’s Mark Hotel Premier Collection Premium Cooling Gel Memory Foam Pillow is under $20. It also has a cool-to-the-touch, washable zip cover with an antimicrobial treatment that prevents odor-causing bacteria from growing, according to Sam's. ","Member’s Mark Lindsey Modular Fabric Sofa with Storage Ottoman","Upgrade your living space with a new place for loved ones to settle in. This plush sofa’s modular design means you can change the different pieces and connect the storage ottoman on either side to create a lounge that fits best in your space or use it as a separate coffee table/footrest. It comes in seven neutral, stain-resistant, water-repellant and pet-friendly fabrics.","Member’s Mark 24-oz Stainless Steel Insulated Tumblers (2-pack)","Available in four color combinations, this set of two stainless steel tumblers can help you up your water intake while cutting down on single-use plastics. The 24-ounce tumblers have double-wall vacuum insulation, which keeps hot drinks warm, cold drinks chilled and the bottle sweat-free, according to the brand. These cupholder-friendly tumblers also come with screw lids and stainless steel straws with silicone tips. Plus, the tumblers are BPA-free, says Sam's, and dishwasher-safe. ","Member’s Mark Set of 2 Acacia Wood Charcuterie Boards","Whether you’re gearing up for holiday entertaining or on the lookout for hostess gift ideas, check out this set of two charcuterie boards. Handmade from natural acacia wood, the rectangular and round serving pieces have a smooth finish and can be used for everything from meats and cheeses to desserts. ","Member’s Mark Weekender Travel Bag","From road trips to gifts they’ll actually use, there’s a reason this Weekender bag is a best-seller. This durable carry-on bag is made of linen and cotton and has a detachable shoulder strap. The roomy interior has a zipper pocket for cosmetics or small accessories and a separate bottom shoe compartment. ","Member’s Mark 700-Thread-Count Sheet Set","These wrinkle-free, 100% Egyptian cotton sheets are quick-drying and offer hotel-quality softness thanks to a high thread count, per the brand. They’re also a great choice for hot sleepers because the cotton material helps regulate body temperature while the bacteria-fighting finish helps keep them smelling fresh, according to the brand. They are available in eight neutral colors, like Soft Silver, Zinc or Washed Indigo and a range of sizes from twin to split king.","Member’s Mark Women’s Everyday High-Rise Ankle Legging","These size-inclusive leggings are made of four-way stretch fabric that’s UPF 50 and wicks away sweat, according to the brand, and they have two functional pockets for under $10. There are seven colors to choose from, and the removable covers are machine-washable for easy cleaning.","Member’s Mark 2-Piece Hardside Luggage Set","This hardside luggage set covers you for long and short trips with a 20” carry-on and a 28” suitcase.
